<div id="review_336448513" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/336448513" />
    <a title="Jannat Bhat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9774522-jannat-bhat"><img alt="Jannat Bhat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590737960p2/9774522.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/336448513?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jannat Bhat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jannat Bhat" href="/user/show/9774522-jannat-bhat">Jannat Bhat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9774522-jannat-bhat?shelf=sad-ending">sad-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9774522-jannat-bhat?shelf=almost-favourite">almost-favourite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer336448513" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12685922218456722853">My Soul to Keep is the third novel in Rachel Vincent’s Soul Screamers series. In the previous two books, Kaylee and Nash met, fell in love and realised the lengths they would go to prove their love for each other. Without giving away the plot, My Soul to Keep is a whole different matter as Nash fundamentally betrays Kaylee and her character is tested to the limit as she must overcome her shock and pain to push forward nevertheless and save the lives of Nash and her father.<br/>My Soul to Keep starts </span>
  <span id="freeText12685922218456722853" style="display:none">My Soul to Keep is the third novel in Rachel Vincent’s Soul Screamers series. In the previous two books, Kaylee and Nash met, fell in love and realised the lengths they would go to prove their love for each other. Without giving away the plot, My Soul to Keep is a whole different matter as Nash fundamentally betrays Kaylee and her character is tested to the limit as she must overcome her shock and pain to push forward nevertheless and save the lives of Nash and her father.<br />My Soul to Keep starts with Kaylee and Nash at a party where a classmate is using Demon’s Breath. It’s deadly and highly addictive and of course, it's from the Netherworld; Kaylee is going to find out just how this dangerous substance ended up in the hands of kids at her school. What Kaylee finds out is shocking and puts her life and those she loves in grave danger. <br />As with all the books in the series, the best character in the book is Tod and I cannot wait to see more of him. I felt every emotion that Kaylee felt throughout the book. Betrayal, shock, hurt, fear… All those emotions are so cleverly written into the story along with a strong sense of being there. The ending was fierce although I expected nothing less from Kaylee; she’s a strong independent young woman and has really grown into her character. <br /> Rachel Vincent has a terrific style of writing, and is able to convey humour, sarcasm and descriptions effortlessly, without weighing down the flow of the story. I’d recommend My Soul to Keep to all fans of young adult, supernatural fiction. Fans of Richelle Mead’s Vampire Academy will love the banshees and demons in this series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12685922218456722853" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1423244184" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1423244184" />
    <a title="Nika" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12763439-nika"><img alt="Nika" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533820069p2/12763439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1423244184?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nika" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nika" href="/user/show/12763439-nika">Nika</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1423244184" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13607641714414063096">Well, well what a turn around. <i> My Soul to Keep </i> certainly is the best installment of the series so far. It´s darker, scarier, deeper and full of mystery and heart break. Perfect October read. <br/><br/>First of all, though I have to rant on about the highly annoying and unfair attitude of darling Kaylee towards Tod. Ahem, hello? The guy is always there to help them, even though he´s putting his life (death?) on a line. Still, every time something goes wrong he´s the first to blame. While for others means</span>
  <span id="freeText13607641714414063096" style="display:none">Well, well what a turn around. <i> My Soul to Keep </i> certainly is the best installment of the series so far. It´s darker, scarier, deeper and full of mystery and heart break. Perfect October read. <br /><br />First of all, though I have to rant on about the highly annoying and unfair attitude of darling Kaylee towards Tod. Ahem, hello? The guy is always there to help them, even though he´s putting his life (death?) on a line. Still, every time something goes wrong he´s the first to blame. While for others means justify actions and certain behavior born from love or concern are considered romantic and selfless, same situations do not apply for him. Instead, he´s left regarded as <i>reckless</i> and <i>dangerous</i>. I´d appreciate some more gratitude and general friendliness for his constant help. Because otherwise I have to permanently label St. Kaylee and Holy Nash hypocrites. <br /><br />Anyway, the story was awesome. It combines the average drug problem youth is confronted with with the Netherwordly danger and craziness. I´m glad the plot took a turn out of <i>happy peppy rainbow world</i> and Kaylee´s perfect relationship gets seriously bumped up, because - surprise - the guy messed up. Big time, this time. I seriously hope Nash has to work for a make - up, because after what he pulled he deserves far more than a punch in the jaw. Frankly, I feel kind of satisfied that my off feeling about them wasn´t that off. <br /><br />Rachel Vincent´s writing and story grows on me more and more with each installment. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13607641714414063096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('N+W+cASkJjMEW4PwFqLptVo14sS5jLghgKaTmd0ZGN7fthp3d77RnAno3a6MJU8petnCffT4kU8o7pUjNlZQnA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U2gueo5OEDPMh8a5tpicUsjqK5YGUGqtD9ugci/jxH67O4p9/VTnnME0mOcsHzrO6AYLL0skQ8Onk6bIxKyMPA==')})
  }

But then I met Justin. In my ravenously hungry state, the agreement he offered seemed a simple on<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText11091130122752235166\" style=\"display:none\">I didn’t think anything could be worse than waking up in the morgue with a note in my hand telling me I’d go on a killing spree if I didn’t drink blood. But then I met Justin. In my ravenously hungry state, the agreement he offered seemed a simple one: I tell no one what I’ve become, and he would allow me to feed off of him.\n\nI thought I could handle his hot and cold antics that made it seem like he wanted me but only as his dirty little vampire secret, until a chance opportunity changed everything. \n\nThe elite Blackburn Academy offered me a full-ride scholarship, if I can pass their grueling trials. With every fiber of my being, I want to be accepted and learn about the vampire lineage I’m now a part of. Justin... has other ideas. She shares her workspace with two black cats (Kaci and Nyx) and her # 1 fan. Rachel is older than she looks-seriously-and younger than she feels, but remains convinced that for every day she spends writing, one more day will be added to her lifespan.<br /></span>
